DETECTOR   (TELES,SI,SI,NAICR) Two triple-counter telescopes were O0137  1   11

FACILITY   (CYCLO,1USAMRY)                                        O0137  1   15 
REL-REF    (O,C0841001,A.M.Kalend+,J,PR/C,28,105,1983) Neutron    O0137  1   16 
           spectra of Al-27,Ni-58,Zr-90 and Bi-209 were measured  O0137  1   17 
           at 90 and 140 MeV.                                     O0137  1   18 
METHOD     (SITA,EDE,TOF) The p, d, t, 3He, and alpha particles   O0137  1   19 
           were identified by deltaE-E and time-of-flight (TOF)   O0137  1   20 
           techniques over the energy range from a few MeV-up to  O0137  1   21 
           the maximum kinematically allowed energies. A total    O0137  1   22 
           of four events (one TOF and three deltaE-E) was used   O0137  1   23 
           to cover the entire energy range.                      O0137  1   24 
ERR-ANALYS (DATA-ERR)  The uncertainty for the experimental data  O0137  1   25 
           are approximately 10 %.                                O0137  1   26
